FILE: tests/metagenSheetSnapshot.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import {
  readHeaderPlusRowsDocument,
  readTableDocument,
  getSheetActualRowCount,
  getSheetActualColumnCount
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/sheetSnapshot.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

function createFakeSheet(matrix) {
  return {
    getRange(startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount) {
      return {
        getValues() {
          const output = [];

          for (let rowOffset = 0; rowOffset < rowCount; rowOffset += 1) {
            const row = [];
            for (let columnOffset = 0; columnOffset < columnCount; columnOffset += 1) {
              row.push(matrix[startRow + rowOffset]?.[startColumn + columnOffset] ?? '');
            }
            output.push(row);
          }

          return output;
        }
      };
    }
  };
}

test('params snapshot uses actual sheet dimensions instead of fixed runtime bounds', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    ['A', 'B', '', '', ''],
    ['1', '2', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', '', '']
  ]);

  const snapshot = readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['A', 'B'],
    rows: [['1', '2']]
  });
});

test('params snapshot trims trailing empty rows and trailing empty cells', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    ['name', 'type', '', ''],
    ['p1', 'int', '', ''],
    ['p2', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', '']
  ]);

  const snapshot = readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.header, ['name', 'type']);
  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.rows, [['p1', 'int'], ['p2']]);
});

test('empty params sheet serializes to stable empty header-plus-rows payload', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    ['', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ]);

  const snapshot = readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: [],
    rows: []
  });
});

test('data snapshot trims trailing empty rows and keeps config columns contract', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    ['BOOL', 'Main', 'x', '1'],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', '']
  ]);

  const snapshot = readTableDocument(sheet, {
    maxRows: 100,
    maxColumns: 4,
    columns: ['Тип', 'Блок данных', 'Имя переменной', 'Значение']
  });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.columns, ['Тип', 'Блок данных', 'Имя переменной', 'Значение']);
  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.rows, [['BOOL', 'Main', 'x', '1']]);
});

test('actual row/column detection returns 0 for fully empty sheet', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    ['', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ]);

  assert.equal(getSheetActualRowCount(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 }), 0);
  assert.equal(getSheetActualColumnCount(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 }), 0);
});

test('params snapshot treats unsupported object-like runtime cell values as empty', () => {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet([
    [{ v: 'name' }, { v: 'type' }, '', ''],
    [{ value: 'flow' }, { value: 'REAL' }, '', ''],
    ['', '', '', '']
  ]);

  const snapshot = readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: []
  });
});


==================================================
FILE: tests/metagenParamsSheetLifecycle.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';
import fs from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';

import { extractParamsDocumentValue } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenParamsSheet.js';
import { getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsContract.js';
import { readHeaderPlusRowsDocument } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/sheetSnapshot.js';
import { createMetaGenParamsTableAutoStyle } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/metaGenParamsTableAutoStyle.js';
import {
  AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND,
  RECOMPUTE_MODE
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/metaGenParamsTableAutoStyleInterpretation.js';
import { extractDataDocumentValue } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenDataSheet.js';
import { extractInstancesDocumentValue } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenInstancesSheet.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';
import { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/app-config.js';

const TESTS_DIR = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const REPO_ROOT = path.resolve(TESTS_DIR, '..');

function createFakeSheet(matrixRef, dimensionsRef, options = {}) {
  const styleCalls = [];
  const onStyleApplied = typeof options.onStyleApplied === 'function' ? options.onStyleApplied : null;

  return {
    styleCalls,
    getRowCount() {
      return dimensionsRef.rows;
    },
    getColumnCount() {
      return dimensionsRef.columns;
    },
    getRange(startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount) {
      if (startRow < 0 || startColumn < 0 || rowCount <= 0 || columnCount <= 0) {
        throw new Error('invalid range');
      }

      if (startRow + rowCount > dimensionsRef.rows || startColumn + columnCount > dimensionsRef.columns) {
        throw new Error('out of bounds');
      }

      return {
        getValues() {
          const out = [];
          for (let rowOffset = 0; rowOffset < rowCount; rowOffset += 1) {
            const row = [];
            for (let columnOffset = 0; columnOffset < columnCount; columnOffset += 1) {
              row.push(matrixRef[startRow + rowOffset]?.[startColumn + columnOffset] ?? '');
            }
            out.push(row);
          }
          return out;
        },
        setBackgroundColor(value) {
          styleCalls.push({ kind: 'bg', startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount, value });
          onStyleApplied?.({ kind: 'bg', startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount, value });
          return this;
        },
        setFontWeight(value) {
          styleCalls.push({ kind: 'font', value });
          onStyleApplied?.({ kind: 'font', value });
          return this;
        },
        setHorizontalAlignment(value) {
          styleCalls.push({ kind: 'hAlign', value });
          onStyleApplied?.({ kind: 'hAlign', value });
          return this;
        },
        setVerticalAlignment(value) {
          styleCalls.push({ kind: 'vAlign', value });
          onStyleApplied?.({ kind: 'vAlign', value });
          return this;
        },
        setBorder() {
          styleCalls.push({ kind: 'border' });
          onStyleApplied?.({ kind: 'border' });
          return this;
        }
      };
    }
  };
}

function createCommandWorkbook(sheet, options = {}) {
  const listeners = [];
  const activeRangeRef = options.activeRangeRef || { current: null };
  return {
    getActiveSheet() {
      return {
        getActiveRange() {
          if (!activeRangeRef.current) {
            return null;
          }

          return {
            getRange() {
              return { ...activeRangeRef.current };
            }
          };
        }
      };
    },
    onCommandExecuted(listener) {
      listeners.push(listener);
      return {
        dispose() {
          const idx = listeners.indexOf(listener);
          if (idx >= 0) {
            listeners.splice(idx, 1);
          }
        }
      };
    },
    emitCommand(command) {
      listeners.forEach((listener) => listener(command));
    },
    sheet,
    setActiveRange(rangeInfo) {
      activeRangeRef.current = rangeInfo ? { ...rangeInfo } : null;
    }
  };
}

function flushDebounce() {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 180));
}

function waitMs(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

function collectStyledRows(styleCalls) {
  return new Set(
    styleCalls
      .filter((call) => call.kind === 'bg')
      .map((call) => call.startRow)
  );
}

function collectSortedStyledRows(styleCalls) {
  return [...collectStyledRows(styleCalls)].sort((a, b) => a - b);
}

function createAutoStyleConfig() {
  return {
    debounceDelayMs: 120,
    maxRecursiveRangeDepth: 6,
    mutatingCommandIdIncludes: [
      'set-range-values',
      'set-range-value',
      'paste',
      'cut',
      'clear',
      'delete-range',
      'insert-range',
      'remove-range',
      'replace'
    ],
    fullRefreshCommandIdIncludes: [
      'insert-row',
      'remove-row',
      'delete-row',
      'move-row',
      'move-rows',
      'move-range',
      'insert-column',
      'remove-column',
      'delete-column',
      'move-column',
      'move-columns',
      'insert-range-move-down',
      'delete-range-move-up'
    ],
    rowCategory: { empty: 'empty', key: 'key', value: 'value' },
    border: { type: 'ALL', style: 'THIN', color: '#000000' },
    rowStyles: {
      key: { backgroundColor: '#eee', fontWeight: 'bold', horizontalAlignment: 'center', verticalAlignment: 'middle' },
      normal: { backgroundColor: '#fff', fontWeight: 'normal', horizontalAlignment: 'left', verticalAlignment: 'middle' }
    }
  };
}

function createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger, onStyleApplied, activeRange }) {
  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, dimensions, { onStyleApplied });
  const workbook = createCommandWorkbook(sheet, {
    activeRangeRef: { current: activeRange || null }
  });

  const controller = createMetaGenParamsTableAutoStyle({
    univerAPI: {
      Enum: {
        BorderType: { ALL: 'ALL' },
        BorderStyleTypes: { THIN: 'THIN' }
      }
    },
    workbook,
    sheet,
    logger,
    source: 'metagen.test.auto-style',
    logMessages: {
      paramsAutoStyleInit: 'init',
      paramsAutoStyleRefreshScheduled: 'scheduled',
      paramsAutoStyleApplied: 'applied',
      paramsAutoStyleFailed: 'failed'
    },
    rowCount: 100,
    columnCount: 10,
    autoStyleConfig: createAutoStyleConfig()
  });

  return { sheet, workbook, controller };
}

test('params extract path keeps single source of truth based on actual dimensions', () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['name', 'type', '', '', ''],
    ['p1', 'int', '', '', ''],
    ['', '', '', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, dimensions);

  const snapshot = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: dimensions.columns });
  const expected = readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows: 100, maxColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, expected);
  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: [['p1', 'int']]
  });
});

test('params auto-style survives row deletion and keeps structured blocks consistent', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 3, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, errorCalls: [], error(...args) { this.errorCalls.push(args); } };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();

  dimensions.rows = 2;
  matrix.splice(2, 1);

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.remove-row', params: { startRow: 2, endRow: 2 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  const blocks = controller.getStructuredBlocks();

  assert.equal(Array.isArray(blocks), true);
  assert.equal(blocks.length, 1);
  assert.deepEqual(blocks[0].keyValues, ['K1']);
  assert.deepEqual(blocks[0].valueRows, [['V1']]);
  assert.ok(sheet.styleCalls.length > 0);
  assert.equal(logger.errorCalls.length, 0);

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style survives column deletion and keeps extracted params shape actual-sized', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['name', 'type', 'unit'],
    ['flow', 'REAL', 'm3/h']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, errorCalls: [], error(...args) { this.errorCalls.push(args); } };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();

  dimensions.columns = 9;
  matrix[0].pop();
  matrix[1].pop();

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.remove-column', params: { startColumn: 2, endColumn: 2 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  const snapshot = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 });
  const blocks = controller.getStructuredBlocks();

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: [['flow', 'REAL']]
  });
  assert.equal(blocks.length, 1);
  assert.deepEqual(blocks[0].keyValues, ['name', 'type']);
  assert.deepEqual(blocks[0].valueRows, [['flow', 'REAL']]);
  assert.equal(logger.errorCalls.length, 0);

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params extract remains stable after structural column shrink under bootstrap maxColumns hint', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['name', 'type', 'unit'],
    ['flow', 'REAL', 'm3/h']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, errorCalls: [], error(...args) { this.errorCalls.push(args); } };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();

  dimensions.columns = 9;
  matrix[0].pop();
  matrix[1].pop();

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.remove-column', params: { startColumn: 2, endColumn: 2 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.doesNotThrow(() => {
    const snapshot = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 });
    assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: ['name', 'type'],
      rows: [['flow', 'REAL']]
    });
  });

  controller.dispose();
});


test('params extract preserves actual expanded dimensions beyond bootstrap defaults', () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['name', 'type', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'note'],
    ['flow', 'REAL', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'expanded']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 130, columns: 12 };
  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, dimensions);

  const snapshot = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(snapshot, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'note'],
    rows: [['flow', 'REAL', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'expanded']]
  });
});


test('params contract keeps leading empty structural row before first non-empty block across extract/rebuild cycle', () => {
  const input = {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: [],
    rows: [['key'], ['value']]
  };

  const dimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions(input, { rows: 1, defaultColumns: 2 });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 3);
  assert.deepEqual(dimensions.normalized, input);

  const matrix = [
    ['', ''],
    ['key', ''],
    ['value', '']
  ];
  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, { rows: 3, columns: 2 });
  const extracted = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 1, defaultColumns: 2 });

  assert.deepEqual(extracted, input);
});

test('clearing first key row reclassifies next non-empty row as key without cursor move', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 3, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  matrix[0][0] = '';

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values', params: { startRow: 0, endRow: 0 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style recomputes full logical block upward and downward for in-block edit', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V3', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 6, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;
  matrix[1][0] = 'V1-edited';

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values', params: { startRow: 1, endRow: 1 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  const styledRows = collectStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls);

  assert.deepEqual([...styledRows].sort((a, b) => a - b), [0, 1, 2]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'key');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style expands rectangular range edit across two logical blocks without full-table fallback', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K3', '', ''],
    ['V3', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 8, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;
  matrix[1][1] = 'x';
  matrix[3][1] = 'y';

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      payload: {
        startRow: 1,
        rowCount: 3
      }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(6), 'key');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style merges multi-area range payload and expands to first/last logical block boundaries', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K3', '', ''],
    ['V3', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 8, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;
  matrix[1][2] = 'a';
  matrix[4][2] = 'b';

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values',
    params: {
      ranges: [
        { startRow: 1, endRow: 1 },
        { startRow: 4, endRow: 4 }
      ],
      nested: {
        area: [{ row: 1 }, { row: 4 }]
      }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(6), 'key');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style recomputes from first affected row to actual end on structural insert-row command', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 5, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  dimensions.rows = 6;
  matrix.splice(1, 0, ['', '', '']);

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.insert-row', params: { startRow: 1, endRow: 1 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(5), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style forces full refresh on structural insert-column command without losing row categories', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', 'meta', ''],
    ['V1', 'meta', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', 'meta', ''],
    ['V2', 'meta', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 5, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  dimensions.columns = 4;
  matrix.forEach((row) => row.splice(1, 0, ''));

  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.insert-column', params: { startColumn: 1, endColumn: 1 } });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style ignores mutating command re-entry emitted during internal style apply', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 3, columns: 3 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    errorCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error(...args) {
      this.errorCalls.push(args);
    }
  };

  let workbookRef = null;
  const { workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({
    matrix,
    dimensions,
    logger,
    onStyleApplied(call) {
      if (call.kind !== 'bg') {
        return;
      }

      workbookRef?.emitCommand({
        id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values',
        params: { startRow: call.startRow, endRow: call.startRow }
      });
    }
  });
  workbookRef = workbook;

  await waitMs(600);

  const appliedCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied').length;
  const scheduledCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'scheduled').length;

  assert.equal(appliedCount, 1);
  assert.equal(scheduledCount, 1);
  assert.equal(logger.errorCalls.length, 0);

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style stays idle after init even when style apply emits mutating commands', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 2, columns: 3 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error: () => {}
  };

  let workbookRef = null;
  const { workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({
    matrix,
    dimensions,
    logger,
    onStyleApplied(call) {
      if (call.kind !== 'bg') {
        return;
      }

      workbookRef?.emitCommand({
        id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values',
        params: { startRow: call.startRow, endRow: call.startRow }
      });
    }
  });
  workbookRef = workbook;

  await waitMs(900);

  const appliedCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied').length;
  const scheduledCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'scheduled').length;

  assert.equal(appliedCount, 1);
  assert.equal(scheduledCount, 1);

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style replay suppression ignores replay write commands and uses one targeted replay refresh', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 3, columns: 3 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error: () => {}
  };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  logger.infoCalls.length = 0;
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  controller.beginReplaySuppression();
  matrix[1][0] = 'V1-replay';
  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values', params: { startRow: 1, endRow: 1 } });
  controller.endReplaySuppression();
  await flushDebounce();

  const scheduledAfterSuppressedReplayWrite = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'scheduled');
  assert.equal(scheduledAfterSuppressedReplayWrite.length, 0);
  assert.equal(sheet.styleCalls.length, 0);

  controller.refreshReplayBounds({ startRow: 1, endRow: 1 });

  const replayScheduledEntries = logger.infoCalls.filter(
    (entry) => entry[1] === 'scheduled' && entry[2]?.reason === 'replay-refresh'
  );

  assert.equal(replayScheduledEntries.length, 1);
  assert.equal(replayScheduledEntries[0][2]?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK);
  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style reopen init styles non-empty rows while skipping unchanged bootstrap-empty tail', async () => {
  const matrix = [];
  matrix[0] = ['name', '', ''];
  matrix[1] = ['flow', '', ''];
  matrix[100] = ['K100', '', ''];
  matrix[101] = ['V100', '', ''];
  const dimensions = { rows: 130, columns: 3 };
  const initialLogger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error: () => {}
  };

  const firstRuntime = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger: initialLogger });
  await flushDebounce();
  firstRuntime.controller.dispose();

  const reopenLogger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error: () => {}
  };
  const { sheet, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger: reopenLogger });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 100, 101]);
  const appliedPayloads = reopenLogger.infoCalls
    .filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied')
    .map((entry) => entry[2]);
  const initAppliedPayload = appliedPayloads[0];
  assert.equal(initAppliedPayload?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL);
  assert.equal(initAppliedPayload?.restyleUnchangedRows, false);
  assert.equal(initAppliedPayload?.styledRowsCount, 4);
  assert.equal(initAppliedPayload?.actualRowCount, 130);

  controller.dispose();
});

test('params auto-style still recomputes on ordinary mutating command with re-entry guard enabled', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 4, columns: 3 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    },
    error: () => {}
  };

  let workbookRef = null;
  const { workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({
    matrix,
    dimensions,
    logger,
    onStyleApplied(call) {
      if (call.kind !== 'bg') {
        return;
      }

      workbookRef?.emitCommand({
        id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values',
        params: { startRow: call.startRow, endRow: call.startRow }
      });
    }
  });
  workbookRef = workbook;

  await waitMs(500);
  matrix[1][0] = 'V1-updated';
  workbook.emitCommand({ id: 'sheet.command.set-range-values', params: { startRow: 1, endRow: 1 } });
  await waitMs(500);

  const appliedCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied').length;
  const scheduledCount = logger.infoCalls.filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'scheduled').length;

  assert.equal(appliedCount, 2);
  assert.equal(scheduledCount, 2);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('cut-like paste into earlier row restyles emptied source tail row even when source row is block tail', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    error: () => {},
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    }
  };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({
    matrix,
    dimensions,
    logger,
    activeRange: { startRow: 2, endRow: 2 }
  });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  matrix[0][0] = matrix[2][0];
  matrix[2][0] = '';

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      pasteType: 'cut',
      startRow: 0,
      endRow: 0
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2]);
  const appliedPayloads = logger.infoCalls
    .filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied')
    .map((entry) => entry[2]);
  const appliedPayload = appliedPayloads[appliedPayloads.length - 1];
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END);
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.logicalExpansionKind, AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY);
  assert.deepEqual(appliedPayload?.bounds, { startRow: 0, endRow: 2 });
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'empty');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('copy-paste mixed rectangular range expands to affected logical block boundaries and keeps row categories correct', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 6, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  matrix[3][0] = matrix[0][0];
  matrix[4][0] = matrix[1][0];
  matrix[5][0] = matrix[2][0];

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      pasteType: 'copy',
      sourceRange: { startRow: 0, endRow: 2 },
      destinationRange: { startRow: 3, endRow: 5 }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'empty');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(5), 'empty');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('copy-paste mixed rectangular range crossing separator restyles lower pasted rows after separator', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 8, columns: 3 };
  const logger = { info: () => {}, error: () => {} };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  const sourceRows = [
    matrix[0][0],
    matrix[1][0],
    matrix[2][0],
    matrix[3][0],
    matrix[4][0],
    matrix[5][0]
  ];
  matrix[2][0] = sourceRows[0];
  matrix[3][0] = sourceRows[1];
  matrix[4][0] = sourceRows[2];
  matrix[5][0] = sourceRows[3];
  matrix[6][0] = sourceRows[4];
  matrix[7][0] = sourceRows[5];

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      pasteType: 'copy',
      sourceRange: { startRow: 0, endRow: 5 },
      destinationRange: { startRow: 2, endRow: 7 }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'empty');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(5), 'empty');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(6), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(7), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('set-range-values mutation with row-indexed cellValue map is treated as range for multi-row mixed paste', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 7, columns: 3 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    error: () => {},
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    }
  };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  matrix[4][0] = matrix[0][0];
  matrix[5][0] = matrix[1][0];

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.mutation.set-range-values',
    params: {
      startRow: 4,
      startColumn: 0,
      cellValue: {
        4: { 0: { v: matrix[4][0] } },
        5: { 0: { v: matrix[5][0] } }
      }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [3, 4, 5]);
  const appliedPayloads = logger.infoCalls
    .filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied')
    .map((entry) => entry[2]);
  const appliedPayload = appliedPayloads[appliedPayloads.length - 1];
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK);
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.logicalExpansionKind, AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE);
  assert.deepEqual(appliedPayload?.bounds, { startRow: 3, endRow: 5 });
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(3), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(5), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('cut-like paste with destination-only bounds refreshes from earliest known affected row instead of full table', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V3', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    error: () => {},
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    }
  };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({
    matrix,
    dimensions,
    logger,
    activeRange: { startRow: 2, endRow: 2 }
  });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  matrix[4][0] = matrix[2][0];
  matrix[2][0] = '';

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      pasteType: 'cut',
      startRow: 4,
      endRow: 4
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [2, 3, 4, 5]);
  const appliedPayloads = logger.infoCalls
    .filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied')
    .map((entry) => entry[2]);
  const appliedPayload = appliedPayloads[appliedPayloads.length - 1];
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END);
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.logicalExpansionKind, AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY);
  assert.deepEqual(appliedPayload?.bounds, { startRow: 2, endRow: 5 });
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.styledRowsCount, 4);
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.actualRowCount, 100);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'value');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(2), 'empty');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(5), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('mixed-range cut-paste with reliable source and destination bounds stays bounded to expanded affected span', async () => {
  const matrix = [
    ['K1', '', ''],
    ['V1', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K2', '', ''],
    ['V2', '', ''],
    ['', '', ''],
    ['K3', '', ''],
    ['V3', '', '']
  ];
  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const logger = {
    infoCalls: [],
    error: () => {},
    info(...args) {
      this.infoCalls.push(args);
    }
  };
  const { sheet, workbook, controller } = createAutoStyleRuntime({ matrix, dimensions, logger });

  await flushDebounce();
  sheet.styleCalls.length = 0;

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.cut',
    params: {
      sourceRange: { startRow: 1, endRow: 3 }
    }
  });

  matrix[1][0] = '';
  matrix[2][0] = '';
  matrix[3][0] = '';
  matrix[4][0] = 'V1';
  matrix[5][0] = '';
  matrix[6][0] = 'K2';

  workbook.emitCommand({
    id: 'sheet.command.paste',
    params: {
      pasteType: 'cut',
      sourceRange: { startRow: 1, endRow: 3 },
      destinationRange: { startRow: 4, endRow: 6 }
    }
  });
  await flushDebounce();

  assert.deepEqual(collectSortedStyledRows(sheet.styleCalls), [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]);
  const appliedPayloads = logger.infoCalls
    .filter((entry) => entry[1] === 'applied')
    .map((entry) => entry[2]);
  const appliedPayload = appliedPayloads[appliedPayloads.length - 1];
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.mode, RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK);
  assert.deepEqual(appliedPayload?.bounds, { startRow: 0, endRow: 7 });
  assert.equal(appliedPayload?.actualRowCount, 100);
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(0), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(1), 'empty');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(4), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(6), 'key');
  assert.equal(controller.getRowCategory(7), 'value');

  controller.dispose();
});

test('data extract preserves rows beyond bootstrap 100 using actual sheet dimensions', () => {
  const matrix = Array.from({ length: 130 }, () => Array.from({ length: 11 }, () => ''));
  matrix[100][0] = 'BOOL';
  matrix[100][2] = 'X101';
  matrix[100][3] = '1';

  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, { rows: 130, columns: 11 });
  const snapshot = extractDataDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, headers: ['Тип', 'Блок данных', 'Имя переменной', 'Значение', 'Комментарий', 'HMI', 'Flt', 'Wrn', 'Alm', 'Trend', 'Conf'] });

  assert.equal(snapshot.rows.length, 101);
  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.rows[100].slice(0, 4), ['BOOL', '', 'X101', '1']);
});

test('instances extract preserves rows beyond bootstrap 100 using fixed two-column width', () => {
  const matrix = Array.from({ length: 130 }, () => Array.from({ length: 2 }, () => ''));
  matrix[100][0] = 'INST_101';
  matrix[100][1] = 'FB_101';

  const sheet = createFakeSheet(matrix, { rows: 130, columns: 2 });
  const snapshot = extractInstancesDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, fixedColumnCount: 2 });

  assert.equal(snapshot.rows.length, 101);
  assert.deepEqual(snapshot.rows[100], ['INST_101', 'FB_101']);
});

test('metagen editor layout composes params | ((data over code) | instances) with three explicit splits', async () => {
  const source = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js'), 'utf-8');
  const configSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js'), 'utf-8');
  const stylesSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/styles/styles.css'), 'utf-8');
  const rightStackClassName = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorRightStack;
  const centerStackClassName = METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.classNames.centerStack;
  const escapedRightStackClassName = rightStackClassName.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
  const escapedCenterStackClassName = centerStackClassName.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');

  assert.match(source, /centerStack\.appendChild\(dataPanel\);\s*centerStack\.appendChild\(codePanel\);/s);
  assert.match(source, /rightArea\.appendChild\(centerStack\);\s*rightArea\.appendChild\(instancesPanel\);/s);
  assert.match(source, /grid\.appendChild\(paramsPanel\);\s*grid\.appendChild\(rightArea\);/s);
  assert.match(source, /Split\(\s*\[paramsPanel,\s*rightArea\]/s);
  assert.match(source, /Split\(\s*\[dataPanel,\s*codePanel\]/s);
  assert.match(source, /Split\(\s*\[centerStack,\s*instancesPanel\]/s);
  assert.match(source, /METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.layout\.outerSplit/);
  assert.match(source, /METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.layout\.innerSplit/);
  assert.match(source, /METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.layout\.rightAreaSplit/);
  assert.match(source, /APP_CONFIG\.ui\.classNames\.editorRightStack/);
  assert.match(source, /METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.classNames\.centerStack/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /topTablesRow\.appendChild\(dataPanel\);\s*topTablesRow\.appendChild\(instancesPanel\);/s);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /Split\(\s*\[dataPanel,\s*instancesPanel\]/s);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.layout\.topTablesSplit/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(configSource, /topTablesSplit/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /createElement\('div', \['metagen-editor-right-stack'\]\)/);
  assert.match(stylesSource, new RegExp(`\\.${escapedRightStackClassName}\\s*\\{`));
  assert.match(stylesSource, new RegExp(`\\.${escapedCenterStackClassName}\\s*\\{`));
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /Split\(\s*\[paramsPanel,\s*codePanel,\s*dataPanel\]/s);
});

test('metagen editor consumes centralized instances runtime and container semantics from config', async () => {
  const source = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(source, /const containerIdPrefixes = METAGEN_CONFIG\.editor\.containerIdPrefixes;/);
  assert.match(source, /instancesContainer\.id = `\$\{containerIdPrefixes\.instances\}\$\{uid\}`;/);
  assert.match(source, /const loggerSources = tableConfig\.loggerSources;/);
  assert.match(source, /const instancesSource = `\$\{METAGEN_CONFIG\.moduleId\}\.\$\{loggerSources\.tables\.instances\}`;/);
  assert.match(source, /const runtimeSuffixes = tableConfig\.workbooks\.runtimeSuffixes;/);
  assert.match(source, /buildWorkbookRuntimeNames\(runtimeNameParts\.instances,\s*documentComponentId,\s*runtimeSuffixes\.instances\)/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /metagen-instances-\$\{uid\}/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /moduleId\}\.table\.instances/);
});

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import {
  getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions,
  normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsContract.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

test('normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument keeps header-plus-rows contract for mixed legacy payloads', () => {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument({
    format: 'legacy',
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: [
      ['flow', 'REAL'],
      'enabled',
      null
    ]
  });

  assert.deepEqual(normalized, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: [
      ['flow', 'REAL'],
      ['enabled'],
      []
    ]
  });
});

test('getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions expands runtime sheet for actual saved payload dimensions', () => {
  const rows = Array.from({ length: 130 }, (_, index) => [`row-${index}`, 'REAL']);

  const dimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type', 'unit', 'group', 'description', 'source', 'a', 'b', 'c', 'd', 'e', 'f'],
    rows
  }, {
    rows: 100,
    defaultColumns: 10
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 131);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, 12);
  assert.equal(dimensions.normalized.rows.length, 130);
});



test('params hydrate runtime dimensions use max of bootstrap and payload rows/columns', () => {
  const dimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type'],
    rows: [['flow', 'REAL']]
  }, {
    rows: 100,
    defaultColumns: 10
  }, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 100);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, 10);
});

  const dimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type', 'u', 'g', 'd', 's', 'a', 'b', 'c', 'd', 'e', 'f'],
    rows: [['flow', 'REAL']]
  }, {
    rows: 100,
    defaultColumns: 10
  }, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.seed
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 100);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, 12);
});


==================================================
FILE: tests/metagenParamsUndoRedo.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';
import fs from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';
import { createMetaGenParamsHistoryController } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsHistoryController.js';
import {
  applyParamsDocumentValue,
  extractParamsDocumentValue
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenParamsSheet.js';
import {
  bindMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeys,
  resolveMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeyAction
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsUndoRedoHotkeys.js';
import { createWorkbenchTabs } from '../renderer/ui/createWorkbenchTabs.js';
import { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/app-config.js';

const TESTS_DIR = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const REPO_ROOT = path.resolve(TESTS_DIR, '..');

function createReplayFakeSheet(matrixRef, dimensionsRef) {
  return {
    getRowCount() {
      return dimensionsRef.rows;
    },
    getColumnCount() {
      return dimensionsRef.columns;
    },
    getRange(startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount) {
      if (startRow < 0 || startColumn < 0 || rowCount <= 0 || columnCount <= 0) {
        throw new Error('invalid range');
      }

      if (startRow + rowCount > dimensionsRef.rows || startColumn + columnCount > dimensionsRef.columns) {
        throw new Error('out of bounds');
      }

      return {
        getValues() {
          const out = [];
          for (let rowOffset = 0; rowOffset < rowCount; rowOffset += 1) {
            const row = [];
            for (let columnOffset = 0; columnOffset < columnCount; columnOffset += 1) {
              row.push(matrixRef[startRow + rowOffset]?.[startColumn + columnOffset] ?? '');
            }
            out.push(row);
          }
          return out;
        },
        setValues(values) {
          for (let rowOffset = 0; rowOffset < rowCount; rowOffset += 1) {
            const rowIndex = startRow + rowOffset;
            matrixRef[rowIndex] = matrixRef[rowIndex] || Array.from({ length: dimensionsRef.columns }, () => '');
            for (let columnOffset = 0; columnOffset < columnCount; columnOffset += 1) {
              const columnIndex = startColumn + columnOffset;
              matrixRef[rowIndex][columnIndex] = values[rowOffset]?.[columnOffset] ?? '';
            }
          }
        }
      };
    }
  };
}

function createLogger() {
  return { info: () => {}, warn: () => {}, error: () => {} };
}

function createFakeElement(tagName) {
  return {
    tagName,
    children: [],
    parentNode: null,
    dataset: {},
    textContent: '',
    type: '',
    tabIndex: 0,
    listeners: new Map(),
    classList: {
      values: new Set(),
      add(className) {
        this.values.add(className);
      },
      toggle(className, force) {
        if (force) {
          this.values.add(className);
          return;
        }

        this.values.delete(className);
      }
    },
    appendChild(child) {
      child.parentNode = this;
      this.children.push(child);
      return child;
    },
    remove() {
      if (!this.parentNode) {
        return;
      }

      this.parentNode.children = this.parentNode.children.filter((entry) => entry !== this);
      this.parentNode = null;
    },
    querySelector(selector) {
      if (!selector.startsWith('.')) {
        return null;
      }

      const className = selector.slice(1);
      const queue = [...this.children];

      while (queue.length) {
        const next = queue.shift();
        if (next.classList?.values?.has(className)) {
          return next;
        }
        queue.push(...(next.children || []));
      }

      return null;
    },
    addEventListener(type, handler) {
      this.listeners.set(type, handler);
    },
    setAttribute() {}
  };
}

function createFakeDocument() {
  const nodesById = new Map();
  const tabsList = createFakeElement('div');
  const editorHost = createFakeElement('div');
  nodesById.set(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.tabsListId, tabsList);
  nodesById.set(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.editorHostId, editorHost);

  return {
    document: {
      createElement: (tagName) => createFakeElement(tagName),
      getElementById: (id) => nodesById.get(id) || null
    }
  };
}

function createDocumentRecord(identity) {
  return {
    moduleId: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId,
    path: `metagen/${identity}.yaml`,
    document: {
      kind: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind,
      component: { id: identity, name: identity }
    }
  };
}

test('params history controller keeps past/present/future semantics and branch cut', () => {
  const controller = createMetaGenParamsHistoryController({
    maxDepth: 3,
    initialSnapshot: {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: ['name'],
      rows: []
    }
  });

  assert.equal(controller.canUndo(), false);
  assert.equal(controller.canRedo(), false);

  assert.equal(controller.push({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name'],
    rows: []
  }), false);

  controller.push({ format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows, header: ['name'], rows: [['A']] });
  controller.push({ format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows, header: ['name'], rows: [['B']] });
  controller.push({ format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows, header: ['name'], rows: [['C']] });
  controller.push({ format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows, header: ['name'], rows: [['D']] });

  const stateAfterPush = controller.getState();
  assert.equal(stateAfterPush.past.length, 3);
  assert.deepEqual(stateAfterPush.past[0].rows, [['A']]);
  assert.deepEqual(controller.undo().rows, [['C']]);
  assert.equal(controller.canRedo(), true);
  controller.push({ format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows, header: ['name'], rows: [['E']] });
  assert.equal(controller.canRedo(), false);
});

test('params replay apply restores header and rows beyond bootstrap limits', () => {
  const dimensions = { rows: 130, columns: 12 };
  const matrix = Array.from({ length: dimensions.rows }, () => Array.from({ length: dimensions.columns }, () => ''));
  matrix[0][0] = 'old';
  matrix[120][11] = 'legacy-tail';

  const sheet = createReplayFakeSheet(matrix, dimensions);
  const snapshot = {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name', 'type', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'note'],
    rows: Array.from({ length: 120 }, (_, index) => [`p-${index}`, 'REAL', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', `v-${index}`])
  };

  applyParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 }, snapshot);
  const extracted = extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 });

  assert.deepEqual(extracted.header, snapshot.header);
  assert.equal(extracted.rows.length, 120);
  assert.deepEqual(extracted.rows[119], snapshot.rows[119]);
});

test('params replay apply path does not create history steps on its own', () => {
  const controller = createMetaGenParamsHistoryController({
    initialSnapshot: {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: ['name'],
      rows: [['A']]
    }
  });

  controller.push({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: ['name'],
    rows: [['B']]
  });
  const replaySnapshot = controller.undo();

  const dimensions = { rows: 100, columns: 10 };
  const matrix = Array.from({ length: dimensions.rows }, () => Array.from({ length: dimensions.columns }, () => ''));
  const sheet = createReplayFakeSheet(matrix, dimensions);

  applyParamsDocumentValue(sheet, { rows: 100, defaultColumns: 10 }, replaySnapshot);
  const state = controller.getState();

  assert.equal(state.past.length, 0);
  assert.deepEqual(state.present.rows, [['A']]);
  assert.equal(state.future.length, 1);
});

test('params hotkey binding intercepts only scoped undo/redo shortcuts', async () => {
  const listeners = new Map();
  const root = {
    addEventListener(type, handler) {
      listeners.set(type, handler);
    },
    removeEventListener(type) {
      listeners.delete(type);
    }
  };

  const events = [];
  let contextActive = false;

  const dispose = bindMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeys({
    root,
    hotkeysConfig: METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.paramsUndoRedo.hotkeys,
    isContextActive: () => contextActive,
    handleUndo: async () => {
      events.push('undo');
    },
    handleRedo: async () => {
      events.push('redo');
    }
  });

  const handler = listeners.get('keydown');
  assert.equal(typeof handler, 'function');

  const event = {
    key: 'z',
    ctrlKey: true,
    metaKey: false,
    shiftKey: false,
    altKey: false,
    prevented: false,
    stopped: false,
    preventDefault() { this.prevented = true; },
    stopPropagation() { this.stopped = true; }
  };

  handler(event);
  assert.deepEqual(events, []);
  assert.equal(event.prevented, false);

  contextActive = true;
  handler(event);
  await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
  assert.deepEqual(events, ['undo']);
  assert.equal(event.prevented, true);

  const ctrlYEvent = {
    key: 'y',
    ctrlKey: true,
    metaKey: false,
    shiftKey: false,
    altKey: false,
    prevented: false,
    stopped: false,
    preventDefault() { this.prevented = true; },
    stopPropagation() { this.stopped = true; }
  };
  handler(ctrlYEvent);
  await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
  assert.deepEqual(events, ['undo', 'redo']);
  assert.equal(ctrlYEvent.prevented, true);

  contextActive = false;
  const outsideContextRedoEvent = {
    key: 'z',
    ctrlKey: true,
    metaKey: false,
    shiftKey: true,
    altKey: false,
    prevented: false,
    stopped: false,
    preventDefault() { this.prevented = true; },
    stopPropagation() { this.stopped = true; }
  };
  handler(outsideContextRedoEvent);
  await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
  assert.deepEqual(events, ['undo', 'redo']);
  assert.equal(outsideContextRedoEvent.prevented, false);

  dispose();
});

test('hotkey resolver supports ctrl/cmd-z, ctrl/cmd-shift-z, and ctrl-y redo alias', () => {
  const config = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.paramsUndoRedo.hotkeys;

  assert.equal(resolveMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeyAction({ key: 'z', ctrlKey: true }, config), 'undo');
  assert.equal(resolveMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeyAction({ key: 'z', metaKey: true, shiftKey: true }, config), 'redo');
  assert.equal(resolveMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeyAction({ key: 'y', ctrlKey: true }, config), 'redo');
  assert.equal(resolveMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeyAction({ key: 'z' }, config), null);
});

test('workbench tabs expose active runtime for top-panel routing', async () => {
  const { document } = createFakeDocument();
  global.document = document;

  const activeEntries = [];
  const runtimeA = { id: 'runtimeA' };
  const runtimeB = { id: 'runtimeB' };

  const tabs = createWorkbenchTabs({
    logger: createLogger(),
    projectManager: { replaceDocumentRecord: async () => {}, renameDocument: async () => null },
    openEditor: async ({ documentRecord }) => (documentRecord.path.includes('a.yaml') ? runtimeA : runtimeB),
    onActiveEntryChanged: (entry) => {
      activeEntries.push(entry?.runtime?.id || null);
    }
  });

  const entryA = await tabs.openDocument(createDocumentRecord('a'));
  assert.equal(tabs.getActiveRuntime(), runtimeA);
  const entryB = await tabs.openDocument(createDocumentRecord('b'));
  await tabs.activateTab(entryB.tabId);
  assert.equal(tabs.getActiveRuntime(), runtimeB);
  await tabs.activateTab(entryA.tabId);
  assert.equal(tabs.getActiveRuntime(), runtimeA);

  assert.ok(activeEntries.includes('runtimeA'));
  assert.ok(activeEntries.includes('runtimeB'));
  assert.equal(typeof entryB.tabId, 'string');

  delete global.document;
});

test('app top-panel params buttons require focused params context and cannot bypass it on click', async () => {
  const source = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/app.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(source, /function getActiveParamsUndoRedoState\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /runtime\?\.supportsParamsUndoRedo\?\.\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /runtime\.getParamsUndoRedoState\?\.\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /state\?\.isContextActive/);
  assert.match(source, /paramsUndoButton\.disabled = !state\.supported \|\| !state\.isContextActive \|\| !state\.canUndo;/);
  assert.match(source, /paramsRedoButton\.disabled = !state\.supported \|\| !state\.isContextActive \|\| !state\.canRedo;/);
  assert.match(source, /if \(!state\.runtime \|\| !state\.supported \|\| !state\.isContextActive \|\| !state\.canUndo\) {/);
  assert.match(source, /if \(!state\.runtime \|\| !state\.supported \|\| !state\.isContextActive \|\| !state\.canRedo\) {/);
  assert.match(source, /await state\.runtime\.undoParams\?\.\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /await state\.runtime\.redoParams\?\.\(\)/);
});

test('metagen editor exposes explicit params undo/redo context state with capability state', async () => {
  const source = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(source, /function supportsParamsUndoRedo\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /function getParamsUndoRedoState\(\)/);
  assert.match(source, /function canUndoParams\(\)\s*{\s*return supportsParamsUndoRedo\(\) && paramsHistory\.canUndo\(\);/s);
  assert.match(source, /function canRedoParams\(\)\s*{\s*return supportsParamsUndoRedo\(\) && paramsHistory\.canRedo\(\);/s);
  assert.match(source, /const isContextActive = isParamsUndoRedoContextActive\(\);/);
  assert.match(source, /isContextActive,/);
  assert.match(source, /isHotkeyContextActive: isContextActive/);
  assert.match(source, /isParamsUndoRedoContextActive: isContextActive/);
  assert.match(source, /isContextActive: isParamsUndoRedoContextActive,/);
  assert.match(source, /if \(!canUndoParams\(\)\) {/);
  assert.match(source, /if \(!canRedoParams\(\)\) {/);
});

test('params sheet keeps toolbar/context-menu visible and hides only native undo/redo entries', async () => {
  const paramsSheetSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenParamsSheet.js'), 'utf-8');
  const simpleSheetSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenSimpleSheet.js'), 'utf-8');
  const configSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(paramsSheetSource, /menu: buildHiddenMenuConfig\(hiddenMenuCommands\)/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(paramsSheetSource, /nativeUndoRedoSurface/);
  assert.match(simpleSheetSource, /toolbar = true/);
  assert.match(simpleSheetSource, /contextMenu = true/);
  assert.match(simpleSheetSource, /toolbar,/);
  assert.match(simpleSheetSource, /contextMenu,/);
  assert.match(configSource, /hiddenTableMenuCommands:\s*{[\s\S]*params:\s*\[[\s\S]*undo[\s\S]*redo[\s\S]*\]/s);
  assert.doesNotMatch(configSource, /params:\s*{[\s\S]*nativeUndoRedoSurface:/s);

  const tablesStart = configSource.lastIndexOf('    tables: {');
  const hiddenMenuStart = configSource.indexOf('hiddenTableMenuCommands: {');
  const tablesSection = configSource.slice(tablesStart, hiddenMenuStart);
  const dataSectionMatch = tablesSection.match(/data:\s*{[\s\S]*?},\s*instances:/);
  const instancesStart = tablesSection.indexOf('instances: {');
  const instancesSection = instancesStart >= 0 ? tablesSection.slice(instancesStart) : '';

  assert.ok(dataSectionMatch);
  assert.ok(instancesSection);
  assert.doesNotMatch(dataSectionMatch[0], /nativeUndoRedoSurface:/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(instancesSection, /nativeUndoRedoSurface:/);
});

test('params replay flow uses suppression and one targeted bounds refresh instead of manual full refresh', async () => {
  const editorSource = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(editorSource, /paramsTable\?\.applyDocumentValue\?\.\(normalizedTargetSnapshot,\s*\{\s*refreshAutoStyle:\s*false\s*}\)/);
  assert.match(editorSource, /paramsTable\?\.endReplayAutoStyleSuppression\?\.\(\)/);
  assert.match(editorSource, /if \(replayBounds\) {\s*paramsTable\?\.refreshReplayAutoStyleBounds\?\.\(replayBounds\);/s);
  assert.doesNotMatch(editorSource, /paramsTable\?\.refreshAutoStyle\?\.\(\)/);
});

FILE: tests/metagenDataContract.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import {
  getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions,
  hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape,
  normalizeMetaGenDataDocument
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenDataContract.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

const TABLE_CONFIG = {
  rows: 100,
  headers: ['Тип', 'Блок данных', 'Имя переменной', 'Значение', 'Комментарий', 'HMI', 'Flt', 'Wrn', 'Alm', 'Trend', 'Conf']
};

test('data contract keeps bootstrap rows as seed but expands for actual rows beyond 100', () => {
  const rows = Array.from({ length: 101 }, () => []);
  rows[100] = ['BOOL', 'Main', 'X101', '1'];

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: [],
    rows
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 101);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
  assert.equal(dimensions.normalized.rows.length, 101);
  assert.deepEqual(dimensions.normalized.rows[100].slice(0, 4), ['BOOL', 'Main', 'X101', '1']);
});

test('data contract normalizes legacy/non-array rows and preserves saved columns fallback', () => {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['A', 'B'],
    rows: [null, 'x', ['y', null]]
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.deepEqual(normalized, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['A', 'B'],
    rows: [[], ['x'], ['y', '']]
  });
});

test('data contract keeps no-op reopen shape for documents already above bootstrap', () => {
  const rows = Array.from({ length: 130 }, () => Array.from({ length: 11 }, () => ''));
  rows[100][2] = 'X101';

  const first = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: TABLE_CONFIG.headers,
    rows
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);
  const second = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(first.normalized, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.equal(second.rowCount, 130);
  assert.equal(second.normalized.rows.length, 130);
  assert.equal(second.normalized.rows[100][2], 'X101');
});


test('data hydrate runtime dimensions use max of bootstrap and payload rows/columns', () => {
  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['Тип', 'Блок данных', 'Имя переменной', 'Значение'],
    rows: [['BOOL', 'Main', 'X1', '1'], ['BOOL', 'Main', 'X2', '0']]
  }, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});


test('data contract hydrate mode uses columns contract width when rows are empty', () => {
  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: [],
    rows: []
  }, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
  assert.deepEqual(dimensions.normalized.columns, TABLE_CONFIG.headers);
});

test('empty persisted data document opens with standard data width instead of 1x1', () => {
  const persisted = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: [],
    rows: []
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(persisted, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
  assert.deepEqual(dimensions.normalized.columns, TABLE_CONFIG.headers);
});


test('empty raw data document uses seed mode and opens with bootstrap row count', () => {
  const raw = { format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table, rows: [], columns: [] };

  assert.equal(hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(raw), false);

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(raw, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.seed
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});

test('normalized fallback headers do not force hydrate mode for empty new data document', () => {
  const raw = { format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table, rows: [], columns: [] };
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(raw, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.equal(hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(raw), false);
  assert.equal(Array.isArray(normalized.columns), true);
  assert.equal(normalized.columns.length, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});

test('hydrate mode still uses actual payload shape for real persisted data document', () => {
  const raw = {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['A', 'B', 'C', 'D'],
    rows: [['1', '2', '3', '4'], ['5', '6', '7', '8']]
  };

  assert.equal(hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(raw), true);

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(raw, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});

test('empty persisted-like data payload with explicit columns opens by columns width and actual hydrate semantics', () => {
  const raw = {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['A', 'B', 'C', 'D', 'E'],
    rows: []
  };

  assert.equal(hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(raw), true);

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(raw, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});


test('empty persisted-like data document still opens with bootstrap row count and bootstrap width', () => {
  const raw = {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: ['A'],
    rows: []
  };

  const dimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(raw, TABLE_CONFIG, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.headers.length);
});

FILE: tests/metagenInstancesContract.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';
import fs from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';

import {
  getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions,
  normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument
} from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenInstancesContract.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../renderer/modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

const TABLE_CONFIG = {
  ...METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.tables.instances
};
const TESTS_DIR = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const REPO_ROOT = path.resolve(TESTS_DIR, '..');

test('instances contract normalizes rows to fixed two-column payload', () => {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows: [null, 'inst-a', ['inst-b'], ['inst-c', 'fb-c', 'ignored']]
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.deepEqual(normalized, {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows: [
      ['', ''],
      ['inst-a', ''],
      ['inst-b', ''],
      ['inst-c', 'fb-c']
    ]
  });
});

test('instances runtime dimensions use max of bootstrap rows and payload rows with fixed width', () => {
  const rows = Array.from({ length: 130 }, (_, index) => [`inst-${index + 1}`, `fb-${index + 1}`]);
  const dimensions = getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, 130);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.fixedColumnCount);
  assert.equal(dimensions.normalized.rows.length, 130);
  assert.deepEqual(dimensions.normalized.rows[129], ['inst-130', 'fb-130']);
});

test('instances contract keeps bootstrap seed rows when payload is compact', () => {
  const dimensions = getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions({
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows: [['inst-1', 'fb-1']]
  }, TABLE_CONFIG);

  assert.equal(dimensions.rowCount, TABLE_CONFIG.rows);
  assert.equal(dimensions.columnCount, TABLE_CONFIG.fixedColumnCount);
});

test('instances config keeps dedicated menu policy source of truth', () => {
  const menuConfig = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.hiddenTableMenuCommands;

  assert.ok(Array.isArray(menuConfig.instances));
  assert.ok(menuConfig.instances.length > 0);
  assert.ok(Array.isArray(menuConfig.data));
  assert.notEqual(menuConfig.instances, menuConfig.data);
});

test('metagen editor consumes explicit instances menu config and no legacy data-menu coupling', async () => {
  const source = await fs.readFile(path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'renderer/editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js'), 'utf-8');

  assert.match(source, /hiddenMenuCommands:\s*tableConfig\.hiddenTableMenuCommands\.instances/);
  assert.match(source, /hiddenMenuCommands:\s*tableConfig\.hiddenTableMenuCommands\.data/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(source, /hiddenDataTableMenuCommands/);
});


==================================================
FILE: tests/editorContextLifecycle.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import { finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition } from '../renderer/ui/editorContextLifecycle.js';
import { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/app-config.js';

function createLogger() {
  const calls = [];
  return {
    calls,
    error(source, message, details) {
      calls.push({ level: 'error', source, message, details });
    }
  };
}

test('table to text/code transition uses shared finalize contract', async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-metagen',
      runtime: {
        finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave: async ({ reason, blockOnFailure }) => {
          calls.push({ reason, blockOnFailure });
          return { continued: true, outcome: 'committed', reason };
        }
      }
    },
    logger: createLogger(),
    source: 'tabs',
    reason: 'table-to-code',
    blockOnFailure: true
  });

  assert.equal(result.continued, true);
  assert.equal(result.outcome, 'committed');
  assert.deepEqual(calls, [{ reason: 'table-to-code', blockOnFailure: true }]);
});

test('context transition falls back to legacy finishActiveTableEditing runtime hook', async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-metagen',
      runtime: {
        finishActiveTableEditing: async () => {
          calls.push('finishActiveTableEditing');
          return 'committed';
        }
      }
    },
    logger: createLogger(),
    source: 'tabs',
    reason: `${APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.menuActionPrefix}${APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.save}`,
    blockOnFailure: true
  });

  assert.equal(result.continued, true);
  assert.equal(result.outcome, 'committed');
  assert.deepEqual(calls, ['finishActiveTableEditing']);
});

test('failed context finalization reports failed outcome and logs once', async () => {
  const logger = createLogger();
  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-metagen',
      runtime: {
        finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave: async () => {
          throw new Error('cannot finalize');
        }
      }
    },
    logger,
    source: 'tabs',
    reason: `${APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.menuActionPrefix}${APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.openProject}`,
    blockOnFailure: true
  });

  assert.equal(result.continued, false);
  assert.equal(result.outcome, APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionOutcomes.failed);
  assert.equal(logger.calls.length, 1);
  assert.match(logger.calls[0].message, /Ошибка завершения редактирования перед сменой контекста/);
});

FILE: tests/projectTreeAdapter.test.js

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/app-config.js';
import {
  TREE_NODE_TYPES,
  TREE_ACTION_IDS,
  buildProjectTreeNodes,
  createTreeBehaviorConfig,
  createTreeInteractionController,
  getNodeActions
} from '../renderer/ui/projectTree/treeAdapter.js';

const MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds;
const UNKNOWN_ACTION_ID = 'unknown-action';

function createProjectFixture() {
  return {
    project: { id: 'project-guid', name: 'Demo' },
    documents: {
      [MODULE_IDS.metagen]: [
        {
          moduleId: MODULE_IDS.metagen,
          path: '/tmp/metagen/a.yaml',
          document: { component: { name: 'Component A' } }
        }
      ],
      [MODULE_IDS.metalab]: [],
      [MODULE_IDS.metaview]: []
    }
  };
}

function createModuleSections() {
  return [
    { moduleId: MODULE_IDS.metagen, moduleName: MODULE_IDS.metagen },
    { moduleId: MODULE_IDS.metalab, moduleName: MODULE_IDS.metalab },
    { moduleId: MODULE_IDS.metaview, moduleName: MODULE_IDS.metaview }
  ];
}



test('tree adapter constants stay wired to config-backed node and action ids', () => {
  assert.deepEqual(TREE_NODE_TYPES, APP_CONFIG.project.tree.nodeTypes);
  assert.deepEqual(TREE_ACTION_IDS, APP_CONFIG.project.tree.actionIds);
});


test('document single click activates existing tab if already open', async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const controller = createTreeInteractionController({
    tabs: {
      openOrActivateDocument: async (documentRecord) => {
        calls.push({ type: 'activate', path: documentRecord.path });
      }
    }
  });

  const documentNode = {
    nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.document,
    documentRecord: { path: '/tmp/metagen/a.yaml' }
  };

  const result = await controller.onNodePrimaryClick(documentNode);
  assert.equal(result.handled, true);
  assert.deepEqual(calls, [{ type: 'activate', path: '/tmp/metagen/a.yaml' }]);
});

test('document single click opens document if tab not open', async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const controller = createTreeInteractionController({
    tabs: {
      openOrActivateDocument: async (documentRecord) => {
        calls.push({ type: 'open-or-activate', path: documentRecord.path });
      }
    }
  });

  const result = await controller.onNodePrimaryClick({
    nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.document,
    documentRecord: { path: '/tmp/metagen/new.yaml' }
  });

  assert.equal(result.handled, true);
  assert.equal(calls.length, 1);
  assert.equal(calls[0].path, '/tmp/metagen/new.yaml');
});

test('module and project node click does not open document', async () => {
  let openCalls = 0;
  const controller = createTreeInteractionController({
    tabs: {
      openOrActivateDocument: async () => {
        openCalls += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  const projectResult = await controller.onNodePrimaryClick({ nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.project });
  const moduleResult = await controller.onNodePrimaryClick({ nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.module });

  assert.equal(projectResult.handled, false);
  assert.equal(moduleResult.handled, false);
  assert.equal(openCalls, 0);
});

  });

  assert.equal(firstDocumentNode.id, secondDocumentNode.id);
});

FILE: tests/tabEditLifecycle.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import { finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch } from '../renderer/ui/tabEditLifecycle.js';

function createLogger() {
  const calls = [];
  return {
    calls,
    error(source, message, details) {
      calls.push({ level: 'error', source, message, details });
    }
  };
}

test('switching away from active tab finalizes pending table edit before activation', async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-A',
      runtime: {
        finishActiveTableEditing: async () => {
          calls.push('finalized');
        }
      }
    },
    nextTabId: 'tab-B',
    logger: createLogger()
  });

  assert.equal(result, true);
  assert.deepEqual(calls, ['finalized']);
});

test('switching tabs does not keep hidden pending state in old tab when no runtime finalizer exists', async () => {
  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-A',
      runtime: {}
    },
    nextTabId: 'tab-B',
    logger: createLogger()
  });

  assert.equal(result, true);
});

test('switch to the same tab is a no-op and does not re-finalize', async () => {
  let finalizeCalls = 0;

  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-A',
      runtime: {
        finishActiveTableEditing: async () => {
          finalizeCalls += 1;
        }
      }
    },
    nextTabId: 'tab-A',
    logger: createLogger()
  });

  assert.equal(result, true);
  assert.equal(finalizeCalls, 0);
});

test('failed finalization is handled predictably by blocking tab switch and logging error', async () => {
  const logger = createLogger();

  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
    activeEntry: {
      tabId: 'tab-A',
      runtime: {
        finishActiveTableEditing: async () => {
          throw new Error('cannot finalize');
        }
      }
    },
    nextTabId: 'tab-B',
    logger
  });

  assert.equal(result, false);
  assert.equal(logger.calls.length, 1);
  assert.match(logger.calls[0].message, /Ошибка завершения редактирования перед сменой контекста/);
});
