FILE: tests/windowCloseGuard.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import { createWindowCloseGuard } from '../main/runtime/windowCloseGuard.js';

test('first close attempt requests renderer confirmation', () => {
  const guard = createWindowCloseGuard();

  const decision = guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });

  assert.deepEqual(decision, {
    allowClose: false,
    preventDefault: true,
    requestRendererConfirmation: true
  });
});

test('close attempt while confirmation is pending does not request renderer again', () => {
  const guard = createWindowCloseGuard();

  guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });
  const decision = guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });

  assert.deepEqual(decision, {
    allowClose: false,
    preventDefault: true,
    requestRendererConfirmation: false
  });
});

test('approved close allows next close attempt without recursion', () => {
  const guard = createWindowCloseGuard();

  guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });
  guard.approveClose();

  const decision = guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });

  assert.deepEqual(decision, {
    allowClose: true,
    preventDefault: false,
    requestRendererConfirmation: false
  });

  const nextDecision = guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });
  assert.equal(nextDecision.requestRendererConfirmation, true);
});

test('cancel close clears pending state and allows a new confirmation cycle', () => {
  const guard = createWindowCloseGuard();

  guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });
  guard.cancelClose();

  const decision = guard.handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed: false });

  assert.deepEqual(decision, {
    allowClose: false,
    preventDefault: true,
    requestRendererConfirmation: true
  });
});


==================================================
FILE: renderer/core/loggerSinks.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const LOG_ENTRY_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logEntry;
const LOG_LINE_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logLine;
const LOG_DETAILS_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logDetails;
const CONSOLE_METHODS_BY_LEVEL = APP_CONFIG.logger.console.methodsByLevel;
const DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD = APP_CONFIG.logger.console.defaultMethod;

export function createDomLogSink({ output }) {
  return {
    write(entry) {
      if (!output) {
        return;
      }

      const node = document.createElement('div');
      node.className = LOG_ENTRY_CLASS;

      const lineNode = document.createElement('div');
      lineNode.className = LOG_LINE_CLASS;
      lineNode.textContent = entry.line;
      node.appendChild(lineNode);

      if (entry.detailsText) {
        const detailsNode = document.createElement('pre');
        detailsNode.className = LOG_DETAILS_CLASS;
        detailsNode.textContent = entry.detailsText;
        node.appendChild(detailsNode);
      }

      output.appendChild(node);
      output.scrollTo({ top: output.scrollHeight });
    },
    clear() {
      if (output) {
        output.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }
  };
}

export function createConsoleLogSink({ mirrorToConsole = APP_CONFIG.platform?.logging?.mirrorToConsole } = {}) {
  return {
    write(entry) {
      if (!mirrorToConsole) {
        return;
      }

      const methodName = CONSOLE_METHODS_BY_LEVEL[entry.level] || DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD;
      const method = console[methodName]?.bind(console) ?? console[DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD].bind(console);
      method(entry.line);

      if (entry.detailsText) {
        method(entry.detailsText);
      }
    },
    clear() {}
  };
}

export function createMemoryLogSink() {
  const entries = [];

  return {
    write(entry) {
      entries.push(entry);
    },
    clear() {
      entries.length = 0;
    },
    getEntries() {
      return [...entries];
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/runtime/projectPaths.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const PROJECT_MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds;
const PROJECT_FOLDERS = APP_CONFIG.project.folders;
const PRIMARY_PROJECT_MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.primaryModuleIds || [];

export function getPrimaryProjectModuleIds() {
  return PRIMARY_PROJECT_MODULE_IDS.filter((moduleId) => Boolean(PROJECT_MODULE_IDS[moduleId]));
}

export function createPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets() {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
    acc[moduleId] = [];
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function flattenPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets(documentsByModule = {}) {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().flatMap((moduleId) => documentsByModule[moduleId] || []);
}

export function getProjectModuleFolders() {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
    acc[moduleId] = PROJECT_FOLDERS[moduleId];
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function joinProjectPath(...parts) {
  return parts
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join('/')
    .replace(/\\/g, '/')
    .replace(/\/{2,}/g, '/');
}

export function getFileExtension(fileName) {
  const normalized = String(fileName || '');
  const lastDotIndex = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
  return lastDotIndex > 0 ? normalized.slice(lastDotIndex) : '';
}

export function stripFileExtension(fileName) {
  const normalized = String(fileName || '');
  const lastDotIndex = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
  return lastDotIndex > 0 ? normalized.slice(0, lastDotIndex) : normalized;
}

export function dirnameOf(targetPath) {
  const normalized = String(targetPath || '').replace(/\\/g, '/').replace(/\/+$/, '');
  const index = normalized.lastIndexOf('/');

  if (index < 0) {
    return '';
  }

  if (index === 0) {
    return '/';
  }

  return normalized.slice(0, index);
}

export function normalizeProjectFilePath(projectFilePath) {
  const normalized = String(projectFilePath || '').trim().replace(/\\/g, '/').replace(/\/+$/, '');

  if (!normalized) {
    throw new Error('Project file path is required');
  }

  const baseName = normalized.split('/').pop() || '';
  if (!baseName || !baseName.includes('.')) {
    throw new Error(`Project file path must point to a YAML file: ${projectFilePath}`);
  }

  const ext = getFileExtension(baseName).toLowerCase();
  const allowed = APP_CONFIG.project.allowedProjectFileExtensions || ['.yaml', '.yml'];

  if (!allowed.includes(ext)) {
    throw new Error(`Project file path must point to a YAML file: ${projectFilePath}`);
  }

  return normalized;
}

export function getProjectRootFromProjectFile(projectFilePath) {
  const root = dirnameOf(projectFilePath);
  return root || '.';
}

export function buildProjectFilePath(projectRoot, projectFileName = APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectFileName) {
  return joinProjectPath(projectRoot, projectFileName);
}

export function getDefaultProjectModuleDirectories(projectRoot) {
  const moduleFolders = getProjectModuleFolders();

  return Object.entries(moduleFolders).reduce((acc, [moduleId, folder]) => {
    acc[moduleId] = joinProjectPath(projectRoot, folder);
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function getProjectOwnedPaths(targetProjectFilePath) {
  const normalizedProjectFilePath = normalizeProjectFilePath(targetProjectFilePath);
  const targetRoot = getProjectRootFromProjectFile(normalizedProjectFilePath);
  const targetProjectFileName = normalizedProjectFilePath.split('/').pop();
  const moduleDirectories = getDefaultProjectModuleDirectories(targetRoot);

  return {
    rootPath: targetRoot,
    projectFileName: targetProjectFileName,
    projectFilePath: buildProjectFilePath(targetRoot, targetProjectFileName),
    moduleDirectories,
    moduleFolders: getProjectModuleFolders()
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: tests/logger.test.js
==================================================

import test from 'node:test';
import assert from 'node:assert/strict';

import { createCoreLogger } from '../renderer/core/logger.js';
import { createConsoleLogSink, createDomLogSink, createMemoryLogSink } from '../renderer/core/loggerSinks.js';

test('logger core respects level filtering and can run without DOM', () => {
  const memorySink = createMemoryLogSink();
  const logger = createCoreLogger({ sinks: [memorySink] });

  logger.debug('test', 'debug message');
  logger.info('test', 'info message');

  const entries = memorySink.getEntries();
  assert.equal(entries.some((entry) => entry.message === 'info message'), true);
  assert.equal(entries.some((entry) => entry.message === 'debug message'), false);
});

test('logger DOM sink renders entries and clear resets output', () => {
  const output = {
    children: [],
    scrollHeight: 100,
    appendChild(node) {
      this.children.push(node);
    },
    scrollTo() {},
    set innerHTML(value) {
      this._innerHTML = value;
      this.children = [];
    }
  };

  const originalDocument = global.document;
  global.document = {
    createElement(tagName) {
      return {
        tagName,
        className: '',
        textContent: '',
        children: [],
        appendChild(child) {
          this.children.push(child);
        }
      };
    }
  };

  try {
    const domSink = createDomLogSink({ output });
    const logger = createCoreLogger({ sinks: [domSink] });

    logger.info('tree', 'rendered', { a: 1 });
    assert.equal(output.children.length, 1);

    logger.clear();
    assert.equal(output.children.length, 0);
  } finally {
    global.document = originalDocument;
  }
});

test('logger console sink mirrors output when enabled', () => {
  const calls = [];
  const originalConsoleLog = console.log;

  console.log = (...args) => {
    calls.push(args.join(' '));
  };

  try {
    const logger = createCoreLogger({ sinks: [createConsoleLogSink({ mirrorToConsole: true })] });
    logger.info('project', 'saved');
    assert.equal(calls.some((line) => line.includes('saved')), true);
  } finally {
    console.log = originalConsoleLog;
  }
});

  assert.match(mainSource, /APP_CONFIG\.platform\.ipc\.handlers\.fsListFiles/);

  assert.match(preloadSource, /const IPC = \{/);
  assert.match(preloadSource, new RegExp(`menuAction:\\s*'${escapeRegex(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.channels.menuAction)}'`));
  assert.match(preloadSource, new RegExp(`windowCloseRequested:\\s*'${escapeRegex(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.channels.windowCloseRequested)}'`));
  assert.match(preloadSource, new RegExp(`openProjectDialog:\\s*'${escapeRegex(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.openProjectDialog)}'`));
  assert.match(preloadSource, new RegExp(`fsListFiles:\\s*'${escapeRegex(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsListFiles)}'`));
});

test('canonical icon contract is PNG-path driven across renderer and menu surfaces', async () => {
  const icons = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets;

  assert.equal('topPanelTitleIconAssetPath' in APP_CONFIG.platform.app, false);
  assert.equal('iconAssetsByAction' in APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu, false);

  const requiredAssets = [
    icons.topPanelTitle,
    icons.panelHeaders.logs,
    icons.panelHeaders.project,
    icons.panelHeaders.params,
    icons.panelHeaders.data,
    icons.panelHeaders.code,
    icons.panelHeaders.instances,
    icons.tree.project,
    icons.tree.disclosure.collapsed,
    icons.tree.disclosure.expanded,
    icons.tree.moduleById.metagen,
    icons.tree.moduleById.metalab,
    icons.tree.moduleById.metaview,
    icons.tree.documentById.metagen,
    icons.tree.documentById.metalab,
    icons.tree.documentById.metaview,
    APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.createComponent.iconAssetPath,
    APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.deleteComponent.iconAssetPath,
    icons.tabs.close
  ];

  for (const actionKey of MENU_ICON_ACTIONS) {
    requiredAssets.push(icons.menuByAction[actionKey]);
  }

  for (const assetPath of requiredAssets) {
    assert.equal(typeof assetPath, 'string');
    assert.equal(assetPath.startsWith('/icons/'), true);
    assert.equal(assetPath.endsWith('.png'), true);
    await fs.access(path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', assetPath.slice(1)));
  }
});

test('menu icon semantics are not duplicated as icon-id maps in config layers', async () => {
  const platformSource = await fs.readFile(PLATFORM_CONFIG_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const uiSource = await fs.readFile(UI_CONFIG_FILE, 'utf-8');

  assert.doesNotMatch(platformSource, /import\s+\{\s*UI_CONFIG\s*\}\s+from\s+['"]\.\/ui-config\.js['"]/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(platformSource, /PLATFORM_ICON_ASSETS/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(platformSource, /iconAssetsByAction/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(platformSource, /menuByAction|panelHeaders|treeActions|tabs:\s*\{/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(platformSource, /MENU_ICON_IDS|ICON_CONTRACT|iconIds:/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(uiSource, /ICON_IDS|MENU_ICON_IDS|APPROVED_ICON_IDS|ICON_CONTRACT/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(uiSource, /iconId:/);
});

test('main menu template uses config-driven PNG paths and does not import iconSystem', async () => {

  assert.match(mainSource, /const menuConfig = APP_CONFIG\.platform\.app\.menu;/);

  assert.match(mainSource, /icon:\s*resolveMenuIcon\('openProject'\)/);
  assert.match(mainSource, /icon:\s*resolveMenuIcon\('closeProject'\)/);
  assert.match(mainSource, /icon:\s*resolveMenuIcon\('save'\)/);
  assert.match(mainSource, /icon:\s*resolveMenuIcon\('saveAs'\)/);
  assert.match(mainSource, /icon:\s*resolveMenuIcon\('exit'\)/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(mainSource, /iconSystem|MENU_ICON_IDS/);
});

test('project export surfaces include png helper and exclude removed iconSystem file', async () => {

  assert.doesNotMatch(exportSource, /assets\/icons\//);
  assert.doesNotMatch(structureSource, /assets\/menu-icons\//);
  assert.doesNotMatch(exportSource, /assets\/menu-icons\//);

  assert.doesNotMatch(structureSource, /renderer\/ui\/iconSystem\.js/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(exportSource, /renderer\/ui\/iconSystem\.js/);
});

test('shared PNG helper is centralized and local helper copies are removed from touched renderer files', async () => {
  const helperSource = await fs.readFile(PNG_HELPER_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const appSource = await fs.readFile(APP_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const staticTextSource = await fs.readFile(STATIC_TEXT_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const treeSource = await fs.readFile(TREE_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const tabsSource = await fs.readFile(WORKBENCH_TABS_FILE, 'utf-8');

  assert.match(helperSource, /export function createPngIconNode/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /export function setNodeIconAndText/);
  assert.match(appSource, /from '\.\/ui\/pngIconRenderer\.js'/);
  assert.match(staticTextSource, /from '\.\/pngIconRenderer\.js'/);
  assert.match(treeSource, /from '\.\/pngIconRenderer\.js'/);
  assert.match(tabsSource, /from '\.\/pngIconRenderer\.js'/);

  assert.doesNotMatch(appSource, /function\s+createPngIconNode/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(appSource, /function\s+setNodeIconAndText/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(staticTextSource, /function\s+createPngIconNode/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(staticTextSource, /function\s+setNodeIconAndText/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(treeSource, /function\s+createPngIconNode/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(treeSource, /function\s+setNodeIconAndText/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(tabsSource, /function\s+createPngIconNode/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(tabsSource, /function\s+setNodeIconAndText/);
});

test('renderer keeps canonical icon contract but resolves file:// runtime src for PNG visibility', async () => {
  const helperSource = await fs.readFile(PNG_HELPER_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const staticTextSource = await fs.readFile(STATIC_TEXT_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const treeSource = await fs.readFile(TREE_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const tabsSource = await fs.readFile(WORKBENCH_TABS_FILE, 'utf-8');
  const appSource = await fs.readFile(APP_FILE, 'utf-8');

  assert.match(helperSource, /export function resolveRendererIconSource/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /location\.protocol !== 'file:'/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /const relativeIconPath = `\.\$\{iconAssetPath\}`;/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /return new URL\(relativeIconPath, baseHref\)\.toString\(\);/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /image\.src = resolveRendererIconSource\(iconAssetPath\);/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /host\.dataset\.iconAssetPath = iconAssetPath;/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /host\.dataset\.iconSize = String\(size\);/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /image\.setAttribute\('width', String\(size\)\);/);
  assert.match(helperSource, /image\.setAttribute\('height', String\(size\)\);/);
  assert.match(staticTextSource, /APP_CONFIG\.ui\.icons\.assets\.topPanelTitle/);
  assert.match(treeSource, /APP_CONFIG\.ui\.tree\.icons\./);
  assert.match(tabsSource, /APP_CONFIG\.ui\.icons\.assets\.tabs\.close/);
  assert.match(appSource, /APP_CONFIG\.ui\.panelHeaderIcons\./);
});

});

==================================================
FILE: main/runtime/windowCloseGuard.js
==================================================

export function createWindowCloseGuard() {
  let isWindowCloseApproved = false;
  let isHandlingWindowClose = false;

  function handleCloseAttempt({ isWindowDestroyed = false } = {}) {
    if (isWindowCloseApproved) {
      isWindowCloseApproved = false;
      isHandlingWindowClose = false;
      return {
        allowClose: true,
        preventDefault: false,
        requestRendererConfirmation: false
      };
    }

    if (isWindowDestroyed) {
      return {
        allowClose: false,
        preventDefault: true,
        requestRendererConfirmation: false
      };
    }

    if (isHandlingWindowClose) {
      return {
        allowClose: false,
        preventDefault: true,
        requestRendererConfirmation: false
      };
    }

    isHandlingWindowClose = true;

    return {
      allowClose: false,
      preventDefault: true,
      requestRendererConfirmation: true
    };
  }

  function approveClose() {
    isWindowCloseApproved = true;
    isHandlingWindowClose = false;
  }

  function cancelClose() {
    isHandlingWindowClose = false;
  }

  function reset() {
    isWindowCloseApproved = false;
    isHandlingWindowClose = false;
  }

  return {
    handleCloseAttempt,
    approveClose,
    cancelClose,
    reset
  };
}
